    require(["jquery","tools"], function (jquery,tools) {
        var dblogin = avalon.define({
            $id: "Login",
            isLogin: false, //判断是否登录
            username: '',
            isfav: false, //判断是否收藏,默认未收藏
            addFav: function (title, url) { //收藏
                if (!dblogin.isLogin) {
                    var mymessage = confirm("请先进行登录！");
                    if (mymessage == true) { //点击确定，跳转登录页
                        window.location.href = "/cspuc/users/login?redirtUrl=http://" + encodeURI( encodeURI(window.location.host) ) + "/cspuc/users/noseLogin?redirtUrl=" + encodeURI( encodeURI(window.location.href) );
                    } else if (mymessage == false) {

                    }
                }

                if (!dblogin.isfav && dblogin.isLogin) {
                    jquery.ajax({
                        url: "/cspuc/apis/collect",
                        dataType: "json",
                        type: "post",
                        data: {
                            title: PageInfo.title,
                            url: window.location.href,
                            random: Math.random()
                        },
                        //jsonpCallback:"jsonpCallback",
                        success: function (data) {
                            //avalon.log(data);
                            if (!data.error) {
                                alert("收藏成功！")
                                dblogin.isfav = true;
                            }
                        },
                        error: function (data) {
                            avalon.log("请求失败！");
                        }
                    });
                }
            },
            canceladdFav: function () { //取消收藏

                var mymessage = confirm("确定是否要取消收藏？");
                if (mymessage == true) { //点击确定，取消收藏
                    jquery.ajax({
                        url: "/cspuc/apis/canceCollect",
                        dataType: "json",
                        type: "post",
                        data: {
                            url: window.location.href,
                            random: Math.random()
                        },
                        //jsonpCallback:"jsonpCallback",
                        success: function (data) {
                            //avalon.log(data);
                            if (!data.error) {
                                alert("取消收藏成功！")
                                dblogin.isfav = false;
                            }
                        },
                        error: function (data) {
                            avalon.log("请求失败！");
                        }
                    });
                } else if (mymessage == false) {

                }

            }
        });

        setTimeout(function () {
            var cspucToken = jquery.cookie("cspucToken");
            if (cspucToken) {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    jquery.ajax({
                        url: "/cspuc/users/isLogin",
                        dataType: "json",
                        type: "get",
                        //jsonpCallback:"jsonpCallback",
                        success: function (data) {
                            if (data.data) { //登录
                                dblogin.isLogin = true;
                                dblogin.username = data.data.user_account;
                            } else {
                                dblogin.isLogin = false;
                            }
                        },
                        error: function (data) {
                            avalon.log("请求失败！");
                        }
                    });
                }, 1000);

                setTimeout(function () {
                    //判断是否收藏
                    if (!dblogin.isLogin) {
                        //avalon.log("未登录状态")
                    } else {
                        //avalon.log("登录状态")
                        jquery.ajax({
                            url: "/cspuc/apis/isConllect",
                            dataType: "json",
                            type: "post",
                            data: {
                                url: window.location.href,
                                random: Math.random()
                            },
                            success: function (data) {
                                //avalon.log(data);
                                if (data.isConllect) { //已收藏
                                    dblogin.isfav = true;
                                }
                            },
                            error: function (data) {
                                avalon.log("请求失败！");
                            }
                        });
                    }
                }, 3000);
            }
        }, 2000);

            } else {
                $(this).addClass('on').siblings().removeClass('on');
                $(this).siblings().children('.mark').slideUp()
                $(this).children('.mark').slideDown();
            }
            return false;   //阻止冒泡
        })

   var w = document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].clientWidth;
require(["jquery","list","tools","dialog"],function($,listModel,tools,dialog){
		var $slideBox=$("#slideBox");

		function IsPC() {
			var userAgentInfo = navigator.userAgent;
			var Agents = ["Android", "iPhone", "SymbianOS", "Windows Phone", "iPad", "iPod"];
			var flag = true;
			for (var v = 0; v < Agents.length; v++) {
					if (userAgentInfo.indexOf(Agents[v]) > 0) {
							//alert("手机端")
							$("#grbs").attr("href","http://zwfw.fujian.gov.cn/cms-app/personal?userType=1");
							$("#qybs").attr("href","http://zwfw.fujian.gov.cn/cms-app/personal?userType=2");
							flag = false;
							break;
					}
			}
			return flag;
		}
				
		IsPC();
	
		tools.tab([
				{name:"Right",index:0}
		]);
			
			//政务公开

											$("#" + key).html(val);

							// if(typeof res != 'object'){

			// 数据统计接口
			function checkSearch(){
					var searchAllKey = $("#searchAllKey").val();
					if(null == searchAllKey || "" == searchAllKey || typeof(searchAllKey) == undefined){    
							var d = dialog({
									title: '提示信息',

									okValue: "关闭",

					}

			// 解读关联
			var zcjdredoc = avalon.define({
					$id: "zcjdredoc",
		docids:"5552357,5551817,5551810,5550467,5550466",
		wjdocids:"5551155,,5548235,5547855,5546961,5546137,5544377",
					redsdocid:[],
					list: [],
					wjreldocid:[],
					list2:[],
					error: false
			})

			function getResList(docids, listarr, type ){ //type: 1 文件 , 2 解读
					$.ajax({ 
							url:"/was5/web/search?channelid="+SiteInfo.was4doc+"&classsql=siteid%3D51*modal%3D1*(docid2%3D"+  docids.join(",")  +")&prepage=20",
							type: "get",
							dataType: "text",
							success: function (d) {
									var str = jQuery.trim( d );
									str = str.replace(new RegExp("[\n\r]","gm"),"");//过滤可能存在的换行
									try{
											s = (new Function('return'+str))() ;//
									}catch( e ){
											( _obj.debug >= debugLevel.error  )&& avalon.log( "ERROR：[model.list.js initListData()]转换文本为对象失败11：" , e )
									}
									for(var i=0;i<s.docs.length;i++){
											for(var j=0;j<listarr.length;j++){
													if( s.docs[i].docid === listarr[j].docid && typeof s.docs[i].docid!="undefined"){
															avalon.vmodels.zcjdredoc.list[j].url = s.docs[i].url;
															//if(type==1){
																	
															if(s.docs[i].url.indexOf("/zcjd/")>-1){
																	//$("#"+avalon.vmodels.zcjdredoc.list[j].reldocid+" span").before("<a href='"+avalon.vmodels.zcjdredoc.list[j].url+"' class='jd' target='_blank'> | 解读</a>");
															}else{
																$("#"+avalon.vmodels.zcjdredoc.list[j].reldocid+" span").before("<a href='"+avalon.vmodels.zcjdredoc.list[j].url+"' class='wj' target='_blank'> | 文件</a>");
															}
														 
													}
											}  
									}	
							},
							error: function (e) {
									avalon.log("请求失败")
							}
					})
			}
			// 政策解读关联
			$.ajax({
					url: "/was5/web/search?channelid="+ SiteInfo.was4rel +"&classsql=(docid2%3D" + zcjdredoc.docids + ")%2B(reldocid%3D" + zcjdredoc.docids + ")&prepage=20",
					type: "get",
					dataType: "json",
					success: function (s) {
							if(s.chnls.length>1) {
									for (var i = 0; i < s.chnls.length-1; i++) {
											if(zcjdredoc.docids.indexOf(s.chnls[i].reldocid)>-1){
													zcjdredoc.redsdocid.push(s.chnls[i].docid);
													zcjdredoc.list.push({docid:s.chnls[i].docid,reldocid:s.chnls[i].reldocid,url:""});
											}
									}

									getResList(zcjdredoc.redsdocid , zcjdredoc.list, 1)
							}
							//avalon.log(zcjdredoc.redsdocid)
						 
							
					},
					error: function (e) {
							avalon.log("请求失败")
					}
			})
			// 最新文件关联
			$.ajax({
					url: "/was5/web/search?channelid="+ SiteInfo.was4rel +"&classsql=(docid2%3D" + zcjdredoc.wjdocids + ")%2B(reldocid%3D" + zcjdredoc.wjdocids + ")&prepage=20",
					type: "get",
					dataType: "json",
					success: function (s) {
							if(s.chnls.length>1) {
									for (var i = 0; i < s.chnls.length-1; i++) {
											if(zcjdredoc.wjdocids.indexOf(s.chnls[i].reldocid)>-1){
													zcjdredoc.wjreldocid.push(s.chnls[i].docid);
													zcjdredoc.list2.push({docid:s.chnls[i].docid,reldocid:s.chnls[i].reldocid,url:""});
											}
									}

									getResList(zcjdredoc.wjreldocid , zcjdredoc.list2, 2)
							}
							//avalon.log(zcjdredoc.redsdocid)
							
							
					},
					error: function (e) {
							avalon.log("请求失败")
					}
			})
			
			// 访谈静态
			var zxft = avalon.define({
					$id: "Sta_zxft",
					list: [],
					error: "",
					showStatic: 1//1读取接口数据，2静态数据
			})
			
			$.ajax({
					url: "/fjdzapp/itv?op=info&id=5dd48fee6a91a2c314c83e52",
					type: "get",
					dataType: "json",
					success: function (d) {
							zxft.showStatic = 1;
					},
					error: function (e) {
							avalon.log("访谈系统已关闭，页面展示静态数据。")
							zxft.showStatic = 2;
					}
			})

			var static = avalon.define({
					$id: "Static",
					//list: [],
					error: "",
					showStatic: 1//1读取接口数据，2静态数据
			})


			function isRun(timeStr){
					return tools.getStatus( timeStr );
			}
			//网上调查
			listModel({
							objId: 'listWsdc',
							Mode: 'advice',
							objArgs: {
											listArgs: {
															chnlIds: SiteInfo.itp4poll,

  <script>
   require(["jquery","tools"],function($,tools){
        /*滚动条滚到一部分菜单固定浮动在顶部*/

        $(window).scroll(function() {
            $(this).scrollTop() > 435 ? $(".nav").addClass('fixed') : $(".nav").removeClass('fixed');
        });
        //新闻tab
        //$(".tit_hov").slide({ titCell:".hd li",mainCell:".bd" });
        
        var w = $(window).innerWidth();
        if(w<=768) {
            //手机版菜单隐藏，点击出现侧边菜单栏
            $('.header-menu-mb').click(function(){
                
                if(!$(this).hasClass('show-nav')){
                    $(this).addClass('show-nav');
                    $('.nav').stop(true,true).animate({"right":0},500)
                }
                else{
                    $(this).removeClass('show-nav');
                    $('.nav').stop(true,true).animate({"right":"-50%"},500)
                }
                
            })
        }

        // 顶部搜索
        var HisString = window.localStorage.getItem("HistoryList"),
            HisArr = [];
        if(HisString != null){HisArr = HisString.split(",")};
        var Rs = avalon.define({
            $id:"list_rs",
            serKey:"",
            keys:[],
            linkKeys:[],
            historyKeys: HisArr,
            error:false,
            showlist:false,
            LockLink:false,
            setPost:function(key,e){
                if( e ) e.preventDefault();
                $("#header form #selecttags").val(key);
                $("#header form").submit();
                Rs.LockLink = false;
                Rs.showlist = false;
            },
            $getLinkKeys:function(val){ //获取联想词
                $.ajax({
                    url:"/smartSearch/interface/word/list.do",
                    method:"post",
                    data:{
                        keyWord: val,
                        siteId : "ff808081624641aa0162476c0e0e0055"
                    },
                    success:function(res){
                        function json(data){
                            var str = $.trim(data);
                            str = str.replace(new RegExp("[\n\r]","gm"),"");//过滤可能存在的换行
                            var s = (new Function('return'+str))();
                            return s
                        }
                        data = json(res);
                        Rs.error = data.error;
                        Rs.linkKeys = data.rows;
                    },
                    error:function(err){
                        // avalon.log(err);
                        Rs.error = err;
                    }
                })
            },
            $togLinkkey:function(){
                Rs.showlist = false;
            },
            $checkLock:function(){
                Rs.LockLink = true;
            }

        })
        Rs.$watch("serKey",function(newVal,oldVal){
            if(newVal==""){
                Rs.showlist = false;
                // Rs.LockLink = false;
            }else{
                Rs.$getLinkKeys(newVal);
                Rs.showlist = true;
            }
        })
        function pushkeys(dataArr){
            for( var i = 0 ; i < dataArr.length; i++ ){
                var item = {
                    keyword : dataArr[i],
                    surl: "/smartSearch/main/search.xhtml?siteId=ff808081624641aa0162476c0e0e0055&key=" + encodeURIComponent(dataArr[i])
                }
                Rs.keys.push(item);
            }
        }

        var defKeywords = ["国家公园","垃圾分类","水质","排行榜","社保"];
        var hotKeyArr = [];
        //
            var keystr = "党史学习教育,政府工作报告,福建代表团,乡村振兴,新高考";
            hotKeyArr = keystr.split(",");
        //
        if(hotKeyArr !== undefined && hotKeyArr.length>0 ){defKeywords = hotKeyArr};
        pushkeys(defKeywords);
        
        
        //一级顶部搜索
        var clickOdd = true
		$('.picker').on("click",function(){
			 var showInput =  $('.picker input');
			 var siteId =  $('#siteId');
			 var isMain =  $('#isMain');
			 if(clickOdd){
				showInput.val('本站');
				siteId.val('ff808081624641aa0162476c0e0e0055');
				isMain.val('');
				clickOdd = false
			 }else{
				showInput.val('站群');
				siteId.val('ff808081624641aa0162476c0e0e0055');
				isMain.val('1');
				clickOdd = true
			 }
		})
		//浮动层定位设置插件
		$.fn.selectCity = function(targetId) {
			var _seft = this;
			var targetId = $(targetId);
			this.click(function(){
				var A_top = $(this).offset().top + $(this).outerHeight(true);  //  1
				var A_left =  $(this).offset().left;
				targetId.show();
			});
			targetId.find("#tagClose").click(function(){
				targetId.hide();
			});
			$(document).click(function(event){
				if(event.target.id!=_seft.selector.substring(1)){
					targetId.hide();	
				}
			});
			targetId.click(function(e){
				e.stopPropagation(); //  2
			});
			return this;
		}
		//调用浮动层
		$(function(){
			$("#selecttags").selectCity("#searchTag");
		});

        avalon.scan($(".ss_box2").get(0));
        // 顶部搜索 end


        //底部链接导航
        $('.yqlj_tit1>ul>li').click(function(){
            if ($(this).hasClass('on')) {
                return
            } else {
                $(this).addClass('on').siblings().removeClass('on');
                $(this).siblings().children('.yqlj_con1').slideUp()
                $(this).children('.yqlj_con1').slideDown();
            }
            return false;   //阻止冒泡
        })
        $(document).click(function(){
            $('.yqlj_con1').slideUp()
            $('.yqlj_tit1>ul>li').removeClass('on');
        })

        // 返回顶部
        $(".fhdb").on("click",function(){
            $('body,html').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 800);
			return false;
        })
    })

  <script>
   require(["jquery","dialog","url"],function($,dialog,urlModel){
        $(document).ready(function() {
            var whiteHost = ["120.35.29.56","120.35.29.200","www.1.cn","www.gov.mo","www.gov.hk","www.fjsen.com","www.crt.com.cn","fj--people--com--cn---z2c50www--fujian--gov--cn.onewocloud.cn","www.fujiansme.com","app3.hxdtw.net","www.eeafj.cn","zqztc.fujiansme.com","220.160.52.171:2022","szfb.fjeec.cn:444","fjaqi--fjemc--org--cn---z934fwww--fujian--gov--cn.onewocloud.cn","www--fjjfypt--com---zb2aawww--fujian--gov--cn.onewocloud.cn","ifc--fujiansme--com---z928cwww--fujian--gov--cn.onewocloud.cn","www--fjscszh--org---za011www--fujian--gov--cn.onewocloud.cn","www--fjredcross--org--cn---ze408www--fujian--gov--cn.onewocloud.cn"];
            function showWarnDialog(url){
                var d = dialog({
                    title: '提示信息',
                    content: '您访问的链接是非政府网站链接，是否继续？',
                    width: 320,
                    okValue: "继续访问",
                    ok: function () {
                        window.open(url);
                    },
                    cancelValue: "放弃",
                    cancel: function () {
                        
                    }
                });
                d.show();
            }
            $("a").click(function () {
                var url = $(this).attr("href") || "";
                var urlObj = urlModel.parse( url );
                if (urlObj.protocol) {    //外链或完整的链接
                    if (/^[\d\.:]*$/.test(urlObj.hostname)) { //纯IP类型
                        if(whiteHost.indexOf(urlObj.hostname) == -1){ // 非白名单
                            showWarnDialog(url)
                            return false;
                        }
                    } else if (whiteHost.indexOf(urlObj.hostname) > -1) {    //白名单
    
                    } else if(url.indexOf("javascript")>-1){
                        
                    } else if (url.indexOf(".gov.cn") == -1) {
                        showWarnDialog(url)
                        return false;
                    }
                } else {  //本站点内连接
    
                }
            });
        })
    })
  </script>
